&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR

- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency

- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Date: Sun, 14 Jan 2024 21:32:12 -0800
Content: Bumps [markdown-it](https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it) from 13.0.1 to 14.0.0.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md&quot;&gt;markdown-it&#39;s changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;[14.0.0] - 2023-12-08&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Changed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Drop ancient browsers support (use &lt;code&gt;.fromCodePoint&lt;/code&gt; and other features).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Rewrite to ESM (including all plugins/deps). CJS fallback still available.
No signatures changed, except &lt;code&gt;markdown-it-emoji&lt;/code&gt; plugin.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Dropped &lt;code&gt;dist/&lt;/code&gt; folder from repo, build on package publish.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Set &lt;code&gt;punicode.js&lt;/code&gt; as external dependency.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Fixed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Html tokens inside img alt are now rendered as their original text, &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/896&quot;&gt;#896&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Hardbreaks inside img alt are now rendered as newlines.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;[13.0.2] - 2023-09-26&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Security&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fixed crash/infinite loop caused by linkify inline rule, &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/957&quot;&gt;#957&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Fixed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Throw an error if 3rd party plugin doesn&#39;t increment &lt;code&gt;line&lt;/code&gt; or &lt;code&gt;pos&lt;/code&gt; counters
(previously, markdown-it would likely go into infinite loop instead), &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/847&quot;&gt;#847&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;
&lt;details&gt;

&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Thread ID: 18d0b9ad9a339ec9
Subject: [MostlyKIGuess/manim-personal] Bump sass from 1.65.1 to 1.69.7 (PR #11)
Date: Sun, 14 Jan 2024 21:31:53 -0800
Content: Bumps [sass](https://github.com/sass/dart-sass) from 1.65.1 to 1.69.7.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Release notes&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/sass/dart-sass/releases&quot;&gt;sass&#39;s releases&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Dart Sass 1.69.7&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;To install Sass 1.69.7, download one of the packages below and &lt;a href=&quot;https://katiek2.github.io/path-doc/&quot;&gt;add it to your PATH&lt;/a&gt;, or see &lt;a href=&quot;https://sass-lang.com/install&quot;&gt;the Sass website&lt;/a&gt; for full installation instructions.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;Changes&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Embedded Sass&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;In the JS Embedded Host, properly install the x64 Dart Sass executable on ARM64 Windows.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;See the &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/sass/dart-sass/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#1697&quot;&gt;full changelog&lt;/a&gt; for changes in earlier releases.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Dart Sass 1.69.6&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;To install Sass 1.69.6, download one of the packages below and &lt;a href=&quot;https://katiek2.github.io/path-doc/&quot;&gt;add it to your PATH&lt;/a&gt;, or see &lt;a href=&quot;https://sass-lang.com/install&quot;&gt;the Sass website&lt;/a&gt; for full installation instructions.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;Changes&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Produce better output for numbers with complex units in &lt;code&gt;meta.inspect()&lt;/code&gt; and debugging messages.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Escape U+007F DELETE when serializing strings.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;When generating CSS error messages to display in-browser, escape all code points that aren&#39;t in the US-ASCII region. Previously only code points U+0100 LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH MACRON were escaped.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Provide official releases for musl LibC and for Android.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Don&#39;t crash when running &lt;code&gt;meta.apply()&lt;/code&gt; in asynchronous mode.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;JS API&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix a bug where certain exceptions could produce &lt;code&gt;SourceSpan&lt;/code&gt;s that didn&#39;t follow the documented &lt;code&gt;SourceSpan&lt;/code&gt; API.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;See the &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/sass/dart-sass/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md#1696&quot;&gt;full changelog&lt;/a&gt; for changes in earlier releases.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Dart Sass 1.69.5&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;To install Sass 1.69.5, download one of the packages below and &lt;a href=&quot;https://katiek2.github.io/path-doc/&quot;&gt;add it to your PATH&lt;/a&gt;, or see &lt;a href=&quot;https://sass-lang.com/install&quot;&gt;the Sass website&lt;/a&gt; for full installation instructions.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;Changes&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;JS API&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Compatibility with Node.js 21.0.0.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;!-- raw HTML omitted --&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;p&gt;... (truncated)&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/sass/dart-sass/blob/main/CHANGELOG.md&quot;&gt;sass&#39;s changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.7&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Embedded Sass&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;In the JS Embedded Host, properly install the x64 Dart Sass executable on
ARM64 Windows.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.6&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Produce better output for numbers with complex units in &lt;code&gt;meta.inspect()&lt;/code&gt; and
debugging messages.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Escape U+007F DELETE when serializing strings.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;When generating CSS error messages to display in-browser, escape all code
points that aren&#39;t in the US-ASCII region. Previously only code points U+0100
LATIN CAPITAL LETTER A WITH MACRON were escaped.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Provide official releases for musl LibC and for Android.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Don&#39;t crash when running &lt;code&gt;meta.apply()&lt;/code&gt; in asynchronous mode.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;JS API&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix a bug where certain exceptions could produce &lt;code&gt;SourceSpan&lt;/code&gt;s that didn&#39;t
follow the documented &lt;code&gt;SourceSpan&lt;/code&gt; API.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.5&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;JS API&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Compatibility with Node.js 21.0.0.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.4&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;No user-visible changes.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.3&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Embedded Sass&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix TypeScript type locations in &lt;code&gt;package.json&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;1.69.2&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;JS API&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix a bug where Sass crashed when running in the browser if there was a global
variable named &lt;code&gt;process&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;

Subject: Re: [sympy/sympy] Fourier Transform not giving Dirac Function (Issue #26053)
Date: Tue, 09 Jan 2024 05:34:54 -0800
Content: See e.g.. https://github.com/sympy/sympy/issues/18855#issuecomment-599059023

-- 
Reply to this email directly or view it on GitHub:
https://github.com/sympy/sympy/issues/26053#issuecomment-1883062082
You are receiving this because you authored the thread.

Message ID: <sympy/sympy/issues/26053/1883062082@github.com>
Subject: Re: [sympy/sympy] Fourier Transform not giving Dirac Function (Issue #26053)
Date: Tue, 09 Jan 2024 06:06:02 -0800
Content: The symbol `i` from sympy.abc is just a symbol with the name `i` and does not represent `sqrt(-1)`. Also it if you want the Fourier transform from `f` to `t` then it is nonsensical to have `t` in the function. The example should be:
```python
In [20]: from sympy import *

In [21]: from sympy.abc import t, omega

In [22]: fourier_transform(exp(2*pi*I*t), t, omega)
Out[22]: 
                âŽ› 2â‹…â…ˆâ‹…Ï€â‹…t      âŽž
FourierTransformâŽâ„¯       , t, Ï‰âŽ 
```
This is the call that should return `DiracDelta`. The inverse transform for this seems to be implemented:
```python
In [23]: inverse_fourier_transform(DiracDelta(omega-1), omega, t)
Out[23]: 
 2â‹…â…ˆâ‹…Ï€â‹…t
â„¯   
```

-- 
Reply to this email directly or view it on GitHub:
https://github.com/sympy/sympy/issues/26053#issuecomment-1883110385
You are receiving this because you authored the thread.

Message ID: <sympy/sympy/issues/26053/1883110385@github.com>
Subject: Re: [sympy/sympy] Fourier Transform not giving Dirac Function (Issue #26053)
Date: Fri, 12 Jan 2024 11:51:36 -0800
Content: In the Inverse Fourier Transform, `omega` and `t` represent the frequency and time variables
``` python
from sympy import * 
from sympy.plotting import plot
from sympy.abc import x, k,t,omega,i,j

delta = DiracDelta(omega - 1)
inverse_fourier_transform(delta, omega, t)
```
Output: 
$` \displaystyle e^{2 i \pi t} `$

and for Fourier transform, 
```python
fourier_transform(exp(2*pi*I*t), t, omega)
 ```
 Output: 
  $` \displaystyle \mathcal{F}_{t}\left[e^{2 i \pi t}\right]\left(\omega\right) `$

--

https://github.com/sympy/sympy/issues/26053#issuecomment-1889866826

Thread ID: 18cfe693c5abbe28
Subject: Get ready for MongoDB 7.0 on your M0/M2/M5 Atlas cluster
Date: Fri, 12 Jan 2024 16:02:32 +0000
Content: Auto upgrade coming soon in February 2024




View in browser 
<https://email.mongodb.com/e/evib?_t=86ba93b39a0e415ea7cd8e8ed81051cd&_m=199da638114b4e5f94a64f553517a72e&_e=qs6N0ztEXzGqQiyrA3NlA_OwkedX8Qbpyn4VHxE7dzD8vZbQh_iZcXYj9taQsdL7>

 <https://www.mongodb.com/>

Hi Mostly,




Your M0/M2/M5 Atlas cluster(s) will be automatically upgraded to MongoDB 7.0 
in February 2024.



Whatâ€™s in the update?

MongoDB 7.0 
<https://www.mongodb.com/blog/post/4-big-reasons-upgrade-mongodb-7-0> 
introduces new features and improvements such as:

 * Compound wildcard indexes 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/manual/core/indexes/index-types/index-wildcard/index-wildcard-compound/>
 * New aggregation operators 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/manual/release-notes/7.0/#aggregation> such as 
$median and $percentile
 * Queryable Encryption 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/v7.0/core/queryable-encryption/> (now Generally 
Available)


What do I need to do?

To ensure a seamless transition, we recommend updating your driver version to 
ensure continued compatibility with your applications. If your applications are 
compatible with MongoDB version 7.0, no downtime is expected for your 
applications. Visit our Docs to seecompatibility changes in 7.0 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/manual/release-notes/7.0-compatibility/>, 
determine whichdriver versions are compatible with 7.0 
<https://docs.mongodb.com/drivers/>, and download the latest version. 



While most upgrades do not require any application changes, if you are 
concerned about compatibility we recommend exploring theStable API 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/manual/reference/stable-api/>.



Not ready? 

You can upgrade to a dedicated Atlas cluster for more flexibility and control 
over when major version updates and maintenance are performed, as well as gain 
access to premium features like point-in-time restore capabilities, automated 
data archival, schema recommendations, unrestricted Atlas search indexes and 
more.



[Upgrade to a dedicated cluster 
<https://cloud.mongodb.com/go?l=https%3A%2F%2Fcloud.mongodb.com%2Fv2%2F%3Cproject%3E%23clusters%2Fedit%2F%3Ccluster%3E>
] 



Questions? 

 Use the chat in the Atlas UI to speak with someone on our team.




Best,

MongoDB Atlas Product Team

- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Message ID: <MostlyKIGuess/manim-personal/pull/3/c1886228325@github.com>
Subject: [MostlyKIGuess/manim-personal] Bump markdown-it from 13.0.1 to 14.0.0 (PR #3)
Date: Wed, 10 Jan 2024 20:35:29 -0800
Content: Bumps [markdown-it](https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it) from 13.0.1 to 14.0.0.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/blob/master/CHANGELOG.md&quot;&gt;markdown-it&#39;s changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;[14.0.0] - 2023-12-08&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Changed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Drop ancient browsers support (use &lt;code&gt;.fromCodePoint&lt;/code&gt; and other features).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Rewrite to ESM (including all plugins/deps). CJS fallback still available.
No signatures changed, except &lt;code&gt;markdown-it-emoji&lt;/code&gt; plugin.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Dropped &lt;code&gt;dist/&lt;/code&gt; folder from repo, build on package publish.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Set &lt;code&gt;punicode.js&lt;/code&gt; as external dependency.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Fixed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Html tokens inside img alt are now rendered as their original text, &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/896&quot;&gt;#896&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Hardbreaks inside img alt are now rendered as newlines.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;[13.0.2] - 2023-09-26&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Security&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fixed crash/infinite loop caused by linkify inline rule, &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/957&quot;&gt;#957&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Fixed&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Throw an error if 3rd party plugin doesn&#39;t increment &lt;code&gt;line&lt;/code&gt; or &lt;code&gt;pos&lt;/code&gt; counters
(previously, markdown-it would likely go into infinite loop instead), &lt;a href=&quot;https://redirect.github.com/markdown-it/markdown-it/issues/847&quot;&gt;#847&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;
&lt;details&gt;

&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Subject: Re: [sympy/sympy] Convolution using Laplace Theorem, and it's properties (Issue #26023)
Date: Tue, 02 Jan 2024 10:59:47 -0800
Content: > So that if they want to take Laplace the code would be shorter and the calculations would be faster too!

Unfortunately, I don't think that the statement that it makes the code shorter, or faster,
(like mathematical techniques to be done by hand)
is convincing enough statement in studies of symbolic computation, or computer science in general,
and may warn that it is not the right direction.

We do may need some improvements about convolution, or laplace transform,
However, I'd recommend you to get some studies about how SymPy does the symbolic integration,
or how to implement the symbolic integrator computationally, to join the discussion in general.

Redesigned the editor UX. A simpler and more efficient interface means less mess
and more attention to what's important. Weâ€™re making unicorn also convenient for
building multi-page websites, instead of only single landing pages.

[https://links.emails.unicornplatform.com/image/process/original/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fcampaign%2Fwebsite%2F7e782a40c0560c00%2Fnewbuilder-1_7cn1m0.gif]


Scroll the page while editing components. Very useful when you have long section
you're editing.


Switch component layout and keep the data. Previous you'd have to remove
component, add a new one and fill all the texts and content into it over again.
Now you can simply switch the component that's used to render section.

Subject: Checkly's Advent of Monitoring: Tips from Our Monitoring Experience
Date: Wed, 20 Dec 2023 12:26:20 +0000
Content: Hi MostlyK, 
 We just completed our Advent of Monitoring. 
 For 12 days in a row, our engineers have been publishing practical monitoring tips from our own experience. 
 In my last email, I shared with you these articles: 
 - The concept of synthetics and why they are needed 
- Debugging dashboard outages with Checkly's API checks 
- Monitoring self-hosted projects with Checkly 
- Solving E2E testing challenges with Checkly's garbage collector 
- Dealing with third-party dependencies causing false positives for synthetics 
- Using Checkly to monitor Checkly 
- Our job monitoring strategy 
 [Image "Prometheus+Metrics+Types-D12.png"] 
 



 
 In the meantime, we also discussed these topics: 
 - Monitoring all the nines of your service-level agreements 
- Multi-step API checks vs. individual API checks 
- Local Clickhouse observability 
- Should you separate or unite testing and monitoring? 
- Using a Smoke Test Matrix to tame variant complexity 
 




 
 Monitoring all the nines of your SLA 
 I want to highlight the insightful article discussing your SLAs and how to ensure that you set a check frequency that reflects how many nines you wish to achieve. 
 [Image "CleanShot+2023-12-20+at+12.17.45%402x.png"] 
 How can we ensure that our service is available for the time we guarantee in our SLA? 
 Read more 
 I hope you enjoyed reading our tips and you implement some of them in your monitoring strategy. 
 Are there any other topics you'd like to read about? Tell us in the Checkly Community Slack - we'd be happy to cover them. 
 I wish you a joyful holiday season that will get you refreshed and ready for the 2024 monitoring challenges. 
 Happy Monitoring, 
 -Hannes

Thread ID: 18c7dd08f2fead4d
Subject: Parallel Check Scheduling is now in beta
Date: Mon, 18 Dec 2023 16:44:28 +0000
Content: Hi MostlyK, 
 I have some exciting news to share: Parallel check scheduling is now available in beta! 
 Hereâ€™s a quick Loom of how this works. 
 [Image "5faea4a31e4b47b2a583e998da4e4282-with-play.gif"] 
 



 
 So far, weâ€™ve had a scheduling strategy of round-robin, where each check is run and executed on a single location. 
 [Image "1702636764427.png"] 
 



 
 Parallel scheduling means that you can choose to run a check from multiple locations at the same time. This will enable you to detect regional outages up to 20x faster than before, depending on the number of locations youâ€™re monitoring. 
 Alerts are sent as soon as a location is registered as failing or degrading, minimizing the amount of time from failure to your engineers being notified. 
 For more information on setting up parallel scheduling, check out: 
 - Our docs 
- Our changelog update 
 Let us know if you have any feedback. 
 Happy monitoring!

Thread ID: 18c7472460649d7d
Subject: MongoDB Security Notice
Date: Sat, 16 Dec 2023 21:04:55 +0000
Content: View in browser 
<https://email.mongodb.com/e/evib?_t=86ba93b39a0e415ea7cd8e8ed81051cd&_m=b2e528d444c54d6ba2477b175e2d01ce&_e=XbGESn0wZLmiXkkk8ghcT-6uGTv5Ep5YwkZmt_fDM6ZiQpJ_wOiYMdEtuYWIrPqu>





Hi Mostly,


 MongoDB is investigating a security incident involving unauthorized access to 
certain MongoDB corporate systems. This includes exposure of customer account 
metadata and contact information.At this time, we are NOT aware of any exposure 
to the data that customers store in MongoDB Atlas. 

 We detected suspicious activity on Wednesday (Dec. 13th, 2023) evening US 
Eastern Standard Time and immediately activated our incident response process. 
We are still conducting an active investigation and believe that this 
unauthorized access has been going on for some period of time before discovery. 
We have also started notifying relevant authorities.

What should you do next?

 *  Since we are aware that some customer account metadata and contact 
information was accessed, please be vigilant for social engineering and 
phishing attacks.
 * If not already implemented, we encourage all customers to activate 
phishing-resistant multi-factor authentication (MFA) and regularly rotate 
passwords.
MongoDB will continue to update mongodb.com/alerts with additional information 
as we continue to investigate the matter.



Sincerely, 

Lena Smart

MongoDB CISO

Subject: Checkly's Advent of Monitoring: Practical Monitoring Tips from Our Engineers
Date: Thu, 14 Dec 2023 20:52:16 +0000
Content: Hi MostlyK, 
 I just wanted to tell you that we launched an Advent of Monitoring series, where our engineers share practical monitoring tips for 12 days in a row. 
 [Image "Prometheus+Metrics+Types-D12.png"] 
 



 
 So far, we've published stories on: 
 - The concept of synthetics and why they are needed 
- Debugging dashboard outages with Checkly's API checks 
- Monitoring self-hosted projects with Checkly 
- Solving E2E testing challenges with Checkly's garbage collector 
- Dealing with third-party dependencies causing false positives for synthetics 
- Using Checkly to monitor Checkly 
- Our job monitoring strategy 
 Stay tuned in the upcoming days, when we'll be posting about: 
 - Monitoring all the nines of your service-level agreements 
- Multi-step API checks vs. individual API checks 
- Local Clickhouse observability 
- Catching issues before they land on production 
- Using a Smoke Test Matrix to tame variant complexity 
 I hope our tips will give you some inspiration on how to improve your monitoring strategy and make your everyday developer life easier. 
 Are there any other topics you'd like to read about? Join us in our Checkly Community Slack and tell us - we'd be happy to cover them. 
 Happy Monitoring, 
 -Hannes

Thread ID: 18c6224bc9eb9572
Subject: Update your security settings to connect to your Atlas cluster
Date: Wed, 13 Dec 2023 07:47:03 +0000
Content: You can quickly connect your cluster by configuring your security settings.



 <https://www.mongodb.com/>

Update your security settings to connect to your cluster 
<https://cloud.mongodb.com/go?l=https%3A%2F%2Fcloud.mongodb.com%2Fv2%2F%3Cproject%3E%23%2Fclusters%2Fconnect%3FclusterId%3D%3Ccluster%3E>




In order to connect to your MongoDB cluster, you must configure your security 
settings. This requires two simple steps and will only take minutes to complete:


1.) Add an IP address 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/security/add-ip-address-to-list/> to your 
IP access list

2.) Add a database user 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/tutorial/create-mongodb-user-for-cluster/#std-label-gswa-user>
 to your cluster

Configure security settings 
<https://cloud.mongodb.com/go?l=https%3A%2F%2Fcloud.mongodb.com%2Fv2%2F%3Cproject%3E%23%2Fclusters%2Fconnect%3FclusterId%3D%3Ccluster%3E>

These settings ensure your cluster is only accessible by authorized users and 
will allow you to start importing and interacting with your data.


See all connection options and learn more by visiting our developer 
documentation 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/tutorial/connect-to-your-cluster/> for 
cluster connection.

Advantages of the document model



Instead of storing data in fixed rows and columns, documents offer a variety 
of advantages, including:



 * An intuitive data model that is fast and easy to work with.
 * A flexible schema that allows for your data model to evolve as needs change.
 * The ability to horizontally scale out.

Subject: Play Christmas songs on piano this year! (Silent Night and more...)
Date: Sun, 10 Dec 2023 09:09:10 -0600
Content: The holiday season really snuck up on me this time around! I've been
getting a ton of requests for Christmas songs, and I've been hard at
work to bring you the best festive piano tutorial content I can
muster.Â 

My hope is that you'll make some holiday magic by playing and singing
for (or with!) your loved ones this year :)Â 

First! Just now I posted a new piano tutorial for Silent Night over on
youtube. This is one of my very favorites, and I teach it in two
different keys so that you can be sure it will suit your voice.

Check it out:

https://echocitymusic.lt.acemlna.com/Prod/link-tracker?redirectUrl=aHR0cHMlM0ElMkYlMkZ5b3V0dS5iZSUyRnFROVgxN0JOdXpZ&sig=DoEn9jTAwWkADHFRPgGJK3NcThiZdNLDLT2szyopXokq&iat=1702221038&a=%7C%7C252571379%7C%7C&account=echocitymusic%2Eactivehosted%2Ecom&email=J4wxPvXX7oxB8J%2F4ESj6D2fRugdksBcNOXkYvM9bele4%2B1qdj0c%3D%3A%2BNfbzz2OPh3yYV8pR7F%2Fr6BjgfDUCX9p&s=a849ca72bd79e8c8e5685de9fe989798&i=13973A14200A5A43439 

Silent Night is the latest addition to my growing Christmas/Holiday
Playlist
.Â 

There are a few others in there from last year, and I will be adding a
couple more in the next week, so keep your eyes peeled!

Also! I find that classic Christmas songs lend themselves particularly
well to teaching yourself by following a chord chart and using a chord
based approach.Â 

This is partly because they often follow a simple form without too many
sections to learn.Â 

Plus, most of these songs just live within us after hearing many
versions of them throughout our lives. Because of this, I don't get hung
up on trying to replicate a specific piano part note-for-note like I
might a famous pop/rock recording.Â 

There is a ton of room to make them your own, be a little creative, or
just keep your playing super simple and let the singing be the main
focus.Â 

Last week I released a video all about teaching yourself songs using
chord charts from Ultimate Guitar.Â 

This approach really shines when it comes to the holiday classics!

Here's that video 

And here are a few song ideas for you to explore using this method:

Jingle Bells

Frosty The Snowman

The First Noel

Feliz Navidad

Hark! The Herald Angels Sing

It Came Upon A Midnight Clear

O Holy Night

Wishing you all the best this holiday season, and I hope your piano
playing can bring some extra joy and togetherness into the festivities.
Let me know how it goes!

All the best

Nate
